[30;1m305 | [0m[35m    and are documented here:[0m
[30;1m306 | [0m[35m    <https://docs.python.org/3/library/enum.html#others> At a glance:[0m
[30;1m307 | [0m[35m      - "is" should not be used at all.[0m
[30;1m308 | [0m[35m      - "format" will return the string value, where "%s" string[0m
[30;1m309 | [0m[35m        formatting will return `NameOfEnum.stringvalue`. Format syntax[0m
